"Colias eurytheme","2014-10-31 00:00:00 -0600","Orange Sulphur (Colias eurytheme) - female

Note: The ID for this female Orange Sulphur was confirmed by Dr. Cliff Ivy, a contributing editor at BugGuide, which is hosted by the Department of Entomology at Iowa State University and may be accessed here: http://bugguide.net/node/view/1183583

31 October 2014: Observed a female Orange Sulphur (Colias eurytheme) nectaring at the Lewisville Lake Environmental Learning Area (LLELA) in Lewisville, Texas. It was nectaring on Blue Mistflower, a wildflower native to the eastern half of the United States. Orange Sulphur is native to North America and as such is an authentic resident of the Western Hemisphere.
